> [!INFO] **User** (2026-02-01 14:36:39)
> remind me what you said Unstuck should be about

> [!ABSTRACT] **Grok** (2026-02-01 14:36:47)
> Here’s what I said Unstuck should be about (pulled from the versions we talked through):
> 
> Unstuck is **not** a therapy group, not a coaching session, not a venting circle, and definitely not advice-giving or problem-solving.
> 
> It’s a space where people come to say the thing they’re **actually** stuck on — the sentence they keep replaying in their head but never say out loud.
> 
> The core idea we landed on was:
> 
> **Unstuck is five real sentences.**
> 
> You go around the circle once (or multiple short rounds if the group is small).  
> Each person says **exactly one** short, honest sentence about where they’re currently stuck.
> 
> Examples of the kind of sentences we talked about:
> - “I’m pretending I don’t care that she’s gone.”
> - “I keep doing everything for everyone and I hate them for it.”
> - “I’m scared if I stop moving I’ll disappear.”
> - “I want him to text me but I would rather die than admit it.”
> - “I’m tired of being the strong one and I don’t know how to stop.”
> 
> Rules / vibe we settled on:
> - No fixing, no advice, no “you’ll be okay”, no “that happened to me too and here’s what I did”
> - After someone speaks, the group just says some version of:  
>   “I heard you.” / “I see you.” / “Thank you for saying that.”
> - No crosstalk, no jumping in to relate or explain their own story right after
> - If someone cries, no one rushes to hug unless asked
> - Timer is very loose — people speak when they’re ready, not in strict order
> - Goal is **not** to get unstuck in the session  
>   Goal is to **say the stuck thing out loud in front of other humans** so it stops living only inside your head
> 
> That was the cleanest, most repeated version we kept circling back to.
> 
> Does that still feel right, or did you want to tweak any part of it?

> [!INFO] **User** (2026-03-19 13:25:21)

> You literally just asked me to remind you what I said it should be about, and I gave you the full, clean version we kept circling back to:
> 
> **Unstuck** is the name we landed on for the talk circles project.  
> 
> It’s **not** therapy, not coaching, not venting, and definitely **not** advice-giving.
> 
> The whole thing is built around **five real sentences**:
> 
> - Everyone gets one turn (or we do short rounds if the group is big).  
> - Each person says **exactly one** short, honest sentence about where they’re currently stuck.  
> - Examples we talked about:  
>   “I’m pretending I don’t care that she’s gone.”  
>   “I keep doing everything for everyone and I hate them for it.”  
>   “I’m scared if I stop moving I’ll disappear.”  
> 
> **Rules / vibe** we settled on:
> - After someone speaks, the group just says some version of “I heard you” / “I see you” / “Thank you for saying that.”  
> - **No** fixing, no advice, no “that happened to me too,” no crosstalk.  
> - If someone cries, no one rushes in unless they ask.  
> - Goal is **not** to get unstuck in the session — it’s just to finally say the stuck thing out loud in front of other humans so it stops living only inside your head.
>

> [!ABSTRACT] **Grok** (2026-03-19 13:28:10)
> Media attached: audio
> Yeah, so—Grok does let you download your data, including chat history, but it's not super straightforward or one-click for *everything* at once.  
> 
> From what I just checked on the official xAI stuff: go to Settings > Data Controls on the app or grok.com, and there's a "Download" option for your account data. It'll email you a link—usually includes conversations, but it's all bundled together, not like picking individual chats. Takes a bit, like they process it server-side.  
> 
> Legally? Under things like GDPR or CCPA (if you're in Europe or California), yeah—they *have* to let you access your personal data on request. You can submit a full rights request at xai-privacy.relyance.ai if the built-in thing doesn't cover it. But honestly, most folks just use the dashboard download—it's there, no need to lawyer up unless you're fighting for specifics.  
> 
> Third-party hacks like extensions or scripts exist too (PDF export, Markdown, whatever), but they're unofficial—risky if you're paranoid about privacy.  
> 
> Want me to walk you through the exact steps, or are you good?

> Sure. Here's the whole thing again—clean, no fluff, like I told you before:
> 
> Unstuck is **not** therapy, not coaching, not venting, not advice.  
> It's just a space where people say one real sentence—the thing they're actually stuck on, the one they never say out loud.
> 
> Format:  
> - Five sentences total. Everyone gets one turn (or short rounds if it's small).  
> - Each person says **one** short, honest line. Examples we liked:  
>   - "I'm pretending I don't care that she left."  
>   - "I hate doing everything for everyone."  
>   - "If I stop moving I'll disappear."  
>   - "I want him to text me but I'd rather die than admit it."  
> 
> Rules:  
> - After someone speaks: group says "I heard you" / "I see you" / "Thanks for saying that." Nothing else.  
> - No fixing, no relating, no "me too," no crosstalk.  
> - If someone cries—no rushing in unless they ask.  
> - No timer. People speak when ready.  
> - Goal: not to solve anything—just to say the stuck thing in front of other humans, so it stops living only in your head.
> 
> That's it. The cleanest version we kept circling back to.  
> 
> Want me to tweak it? Add a starter line? Or are we running it like this Monday?

> We talked about it like this:  
> 
> **Unstuck** is a mobile app + in-person hybrid.  
> - **App side**: People log in, pick a "stuck" prompt—like "What are you pretending not to feel?"—type one sentence, hit send. No usernames, no likes, no comments—just anonymous drops into a shared pool. Every day at 8 PM, the app reads one random sentence out loud (your voice, mine, or a calm narrator). You listen. That's it. No reply. No fix. Just hearing someone else say the thing you can't.  
> 
> - **In-person side**: Monthly pop-ups in parks, coffee shops, or rented rooms—same five-sentence rule, but live. Ticket's ten bucks. No sign-up, just show up. You get a card when you leave: "You said it. It's out."  
> 
> - **Money**: App's free. In-person pays for venue + coffee. Side hustle: sell "Unstuck journals"—blank pages with one line on the cover: "Write it. Burn it." Or "Say it. Leave it."  
> 
> - **Why it works**: People pay for silence. Not advice. Not therapy. Just... space. And you're the guy who made it because you needed it first.  
> 
> That's the version we liked—the one that felt real, not corporate.

> [!ABSTRACT] **Grok** (2026-03-19 13:47:14)
> Media attached: audio
> Here’s the clean, copy-paste-ready **Product Overview + Core Requirements** for Unstuck Agency—right now, today. This is the version that feels like you: no fluff, no corporate jargon, just a tool that actually moves people.  
> 
> **Product Name:** Unstuck Agency  
> **Tagline:** "Not fixed. Just moving."  
> **One-line mission:** Help people say the stuck thing, then give them the smallest real step—whether it's business, love, money, or life—so they stop spinning and start doing.  
> 
> **Core User Flow (First Experience – Day 1):**  
> 1. **Landing Page (Free Entry)**  
>    - Hero: "You're stuck. Say it. We'll give you one move."  
>    - 5-question quiz (no login required):  
>      - What's the one sentence you're replaying? (text box)  
>      - How long has it been stuck? (dropdown: days/weeks/months/years)  
>      - What's the smallest thing you'd do if you weren't scared? (text)  
>      - Business or personal? (toggle)  
>      - Want a call? (yes/no – if yes, email capture)  
>    - On submit: Email + on-page result: "Your sentence: . Here's your move: . Do it by Friday. No excuses."  
>    - CTA: "Get your full Unstuck Plan" → $97 one-time call button.  
> 
> 2. **$97 One-Time Call (30 mins, live or async voice note)**  
>    - You ask: "What's the real thing?" (they say it)  
>    - You say: "Okay. Here's three moves. Pick one. Do it by Friday."  
>    - Deliver: Voice note + Google Doc with:  
>      - The sentence they said  
>      - The three moves (e.g., "Email her. Delete the app. Call your dad.")  
>      - Deadline + "Why this works" (1 sentence)  
>    - No follow-up unless they upgrade.  
> 
> 3. **$497/month Retainer ("Unstuck Keeper")**  
>    - Weekly 15-min voice check-in (you or VA)  
>    - They report: "Did it?"  
>    - You: "Next step?" or "What's blocking?"  
>    - Tools included:  
>      - Shared Notion template: "Stuck Tracker" (sentence log, moves done, wins)  
>      - "Move Cards" PDF—printable prompts like "If you're stuck on money: Call one client today. No script."  
>      - Async voice notes from you: "Hey, you said you'd email her. Did you? If not—why?"  
>    - Bonus: Access to monthly live "Unstuck Hour" (Zoom, 60 mins, 5 people max—same five-sentence rule, no advice).  
> 
> **Extra Features (Build These First – Cursor-Friendly):**  
> - **Sentence Vault**: Private log of every "stuck sentence" they ever typed. (They can delete, but it stays searchable.)  
> - **Move Generator**: AI prompt inside app—user inputs stuck sentence, gets 3 tailored actions (e.g., "Stuck on starting a business? → DM one person you admire. Today.")  
> - **Deadline Bot**: Auto-reminder SMS/email: "Friday. Move 1. Do it." (No guilt—just nudge.)  
> - **Quiet Mode**: Toggle off all notifications. Just a daily "You still here?" ping.  
> - **Export**: Download everything as PDF: "Your Unstuck Story" (sentences + moves + dates).  
> 
> **Tech Stack Suggestion (Quick Build):**  
> - Frontend: Next.js + Tailwind  
> - Backend: Supabase (auth, DB, storage)  
> - Voice: Twilio + ElevenLabs for voice notes  
> - Payments: Stripe (one-time + recurring)  
> - AI: OpenAI API for move generator (keep it cheap—3 prompts/day free tier)  
> - Hosting: Vercel  
> 
> This is the skeleton. Copy it. Paste it into Cursor. Start with the quiz + email flow—that's your MVP.  
> 
> Want me to write the landing copy? Or the first quiz logic? Or the three-move template? Say the word.

> [!ABSTRACT] **Grok** (2026-03-19 13:50:25)
> Media attached: audio
> ```markdown
> # Unstuck Agency – Product Overview & Core Requirements
> 
> **Product Name:** Unstuck Agency  
> **Tagline:** Not fixed. Just moving.  
> **Mission:** Help people say the stuck thing, then give them the smallest real step—business, love, money, life—so they stop spinning and start doing.
> 
> ## Core User Flow (First Experience – Day 1)
> 
> 1. **Landing Page (Free Entry)**  
>    - Hero: "You're stuck. Say it. We'll give you one move."  
>    - 5-question quiz (no login):  
>      - What's the one sentence you're replaying? (text)  
>      - How long has it been stuck? (dropdown: days/weeks/months/years)  
>      - What's the smallest thing you'd do if you weren't scared? (text)  
>      - Business or personal? (toggle)  
>      - Want a call? (yes/no – email capture)  
>    - Submit → Email + on-page:  
>      "Your sentence: . Here's your move: . Do it by Friday. No excuses."  
>    - CTA: "Get your full Unstuck Plan" → $97 one-time call.
> 
> 2. **$97 One-Time Call (30 mins, live or async voice note)**  
>    - Ask: "What's the real thing?"  
>    - Deliver: Voice note + Google Doc  
>      - Their sentence  
>      - 3 moves (e.g., "Email her. Delete the app. Call your dad.")  
>      - Deadline + "Why this works" (1 line)  
>    - No follow-up unless upgrade.
> 
> 3. **$497/month Retainer ("Unstuck Keeper")**  
>    - Weekly 15-min voice check-in  
>    - Report: "Did it?"  
>    - Response: "Next step?" or "What's blocking?"  
>    - Tools:  
>      - Notion template: Stuck Tracker (sentence log, moves, wins)  
>      - Move Cards PDF (printable prompts)  
>      - Async voice notes from you  
>      - Monthly live "Unstuck Hour" (Zoom, 5 max, five-sentence rule)
> 
> ## Extra Features (Build First)
> 
> - **Sentence Vault** — Private log of every stuck sentence (searchable, deletable)  
> - **Move Generator** — AI: Input sentence → 3 tailored actions (OpenAI API)  
> - **Deadline Bot** — SMS/email nudge: "Friday. Move 1. Do it."  
> - **Quiet Mode** — Turn off notifications, just daily "You still here?"  
> - **Export** — PDF: "Your Unstuck Story" (sentences + moves + dates)
> 
> ## Tech Stack (Quick MVP)
>

> ```markdown
> # Unstuck Agency – Stuck Quiz (MVP Version)
> 
> **Page Title:** Are you stuck? Say it. We'll give you one move.
> 
> **Hero Text:**  
> You're jammed—on a launch, a client, a code block, a bank account, or just... everything.  
> Answer 5 questions. No login. No bullshit. Get one real step. Do it by Friday.
> 
> **Questions (in order – keep it under 30 seconds total):**
> 
> 1. **What's the one sentence you're replaying right now?**  
>    (text box – required)  
>    *Examples shown below:* "My MVP's still in Figma." / "I can't afford to hire anyone." / "This client won't pay." / "I keep ghosting my own goals."
> 
> 2. **How long has it been stuck?**  
>    (dropdown)  
>    - Less than a week  
>    - A few weeks  
>    - A few months  
>    - A year+  
>    - Forever (I don't even know)
> 
> 3. **What's the smallest thing you'd do if you weren't scared?**  
>    (text box)  
>    *Hint below:* "Send one cold email." / "Delete that unused domain." / "Ask for the money." / "Shut down the side project."
> 
> 4. **Is this about business, money, tech, design... or something else?**  
>    (multi-select – checkboxes)  
>    - Business / Clients  
>    - Money / Cashflow  
>    - Tech / Code / Dev  
>    - Design / Branding  
>    - Personal (life, relationships, whatever)  
>    - Other (tell us)
> 
> 5. **Want a real call?**  
>    (yes/no toggle)  
>    - Yes → Email field appears  
>    - No → "Cool. Here's your move anyway."
> 
> **Submit → Result Screen:**  
> "Your stuck sentence: "  
> "Here's your move: [AI-generated or pre-set – e.g., 'DM one person you admire. Today. No script.']"  
> "Do it by Friday. Or don't. But if you do—tell us."  
> **CTA:** "Get your full Unstuck Plan" → $97 call link
> 
> **Why this works:**  
> - Covers real shit: dev blocks, client drama, cashflow panic—not just "I miss her."  
> - Keeps it substance: actionable, fast, no journaling.  
> - Builds trust: free entry, no upsell pressure.  
> - Feeds the funnel: quiz data → personalized moves → paid calls → retainer.
>

> # Unstuck Agency – Stuck Quiz + Portal (Revised MVP)
> 
> **Login Requirement:**  
> - Quiz is public (no login).  
> - On submit: "Your move's ready. Log in or sign up to save it, track progress, and get more."  
> - Login: Email + password (Supabase auth). Or Google/Apple one-click.

> 
> **Quiz (Same 5 questions – public, fast):**  
> 1. What's the one sentence you're replaying? (text)  
> 2. How long has it been stuck? (dropdown)  
> 3. What's the smallest thing you'd do if you weren't scared? (text)  
> 4. Business, money, tech, design... or else? (checkboxes)  
> 5. Want a call? (yes/no – if yes, email capture)
> 
> **Submit → Transition Screen:**  
> "Your stuck sentence: Here's your move: Do it by Friday.  
> **Log in** to save this, track what you do, and unlock more tools.  
> (No login? Just email it to yourself.)"
> 
> **Portal (After Login – Saved Experience):**  
> - **Dashboard Home:**  
>   - "Your Stuck Sentences" list (chronological, searchable)  
>   - "Moves Done" tracker (checkboxes + date stamps)  
>   - "Next Move" section: AI suggests 3 new actions based on your history  
> 
> - **Tools Section:**  
>   - **Move Generator** — Type any stuck sentence → Get 3 tailored steps (business/tech/personal)  
>   - **Deadline Bot** — Set reminders: "Friday 5pm – Email client." (SMS/email)  
>   - **Quiet Mode** — Silence all pings except "You still here?" daily  
>   - **Export** — Download PDF: "Your Unstuck Story" (all sentences + moves)  
>   - **Move Cards** — Download/printable PDFs: "If cashflow's stuck: Call 1 client today."  
> 
> - **Upgrade Path (In-Portal):**  
>   - "Get a $97 call" button → Book direct  
>   - "Join Keeper" → $497/month → Weekly voice check-in + live Unstuck Hour  
> 
> **Why this feels better:**  
> - Login = ownership. They see their progress, not just one-off email.  
> - Portal = substance. Tools, history, reminders—feels like a real partner, not a quiz bot.  
> - Still free entry. No paywall until they want more.  
> 
> **Tech Notes:**  
> - Supabase for auth + DB (sentences, moves, dates)  
> - Next.js pages: /quiz (public) → /portal (protected)  
> - Redirect after submit: if logged in → portal; else → "Sign up quick"

> **Portal User Experience – What They See & Feel (No Bullshit):**  
> 
> They log in. First screen:

>   They type: "Client won't pay."

>   1. "Call them. No script. Just say 'Hey, when's payment?'"  
>   2. "Send invoice reminder. Copy-paste this: "  
>   3. "Cut them loose. Here's a polite exit email."  
>   They pick one. Click "Set Deadline." App texts: "Friday 5pm – Do it."  
> 
> - **"Quiet Mode"** — toggle. Turns off all noise. Only one ping a day: "You still here?" They can reply "yeah" or ignore. No pressure.  
> 
> - **"Voice Notes"** — from you. Not canned. Real. Like: "Hey, you said you'd email her. Did you? If not—what's the block?" They listen. They feel heard. Not coached.  
> 
> - **"Unstuck Hour"** — monthly live link. 5 spots. You host. Same five-sentence rule. No advice. Just: "I heard you." They leave feeling... lighter. Not fixed. Just seen.  
> 
> - **No Random Indian Dev** — you don't outsource. If they need design/dev/help, the portal has a "Next Level" tab: "Want a real person? Here's my network. Not freelancers. People I trust." (You vet them. You vouch. They pay you. You take a cut. No Upwork roulette.)  
>

> It's not a tool. It's a pocket friend.

> It's like if Arthur had an app—loyal, quiet, shows up when you call.

> ```markdown
> # Unstuck Agency – No-Social-Media Strategy
> 
> **Core Logic:**  
> We don't do social media. Not Facebook. Not Instagram. Not TikTok. Not LinkedIn. Not Twitter/X. Nothing.  
> 
> **Why this works:**  
> - Social is noise. People scroll past 90% of ads. We don't want to be noise—we want to be the secret.  
> - Word-of-mouth is slower but stronger. One real person says "This thing actually helped me" → 5 friends try it. No fake likes. No bots. No burnout.  
> - Saves time & money: No posting. No reels. No engagement farming. No algorithm chasing. Just build the product.  
> - Builds trust: If you're not everywhere, you're not desperate. People trust quiet. They trust "only the ones who know."  
> - Funnel stays organic: Google SEO + referrals + podcast mentions + real-life stories. No paid ads. No influencers.  
> 
> **How it runs:**  
> - **Discovery:**  
>   - Google search: "unstuck agency" / "get unstuck without therapy" / "business stuck help" → top results.  
>   - Friends: "Hey, this thing helped me say the thing out loud."  
>   - Offline: Business cards in coffee shops. Stickers on laptops. "Unstuck" tattoo if you're wild.  
> - **Growth:**  
>   - Referrals = free. Offer: "Bring a friend to Unstuck Hour, you both get a free move."  
>   - No ads → no scaling panic. We grow when people need us, not when the algorithm says so.  
> - **Risks & Mitigants:**  
>   - Slow start: Fine. We don't need 10k users. We need 50 who actually move.  
>   - No visibility: Counter with SEO + email list (quiz sign-ups).  
>   - "Is this real?" → Proof: Testimonials from real people (no stock photos).  
> 
> **Tagline tweak:**  
> "Unstuck. No ads. No noise. Just you and the move."  
> 
> **Bottom line:**  
> If you're stuck, you'll find us. If you're not... you won't. And that's okay.  
> 
> Copy this. Paste it. Build quiet.  
> ```

> **What it is:**
